2025-10-01T23:53:32.4957420Z [36;1m[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4958060Z [36;1m  while [ $attempt -le $max_attempts ]; do[0m

2025-10-01T23:53:32.4959930Z [36;1m      --entitlements src/build/osx/entitlements.plist \[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4960980Z [36;1m      --sign "$CODESIGN_IDENTITY" "$target" 2>&1; then[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4961840Z [36;1m      return 0[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4962790Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4963450Z [36;1m[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4964100Z [36;1m    if [ $attempt -lt $max_attempts ]; then[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4965290Z [36;1m      echo "Codesign attempt $attempt failed for $target, retrying in ${wait_time}s..."[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4966550Z [36;1m      sleep $wait_time[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4967340Z [36;1m      wait_time=$((wait_time * 2))[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4968920Z [36;1m      attempt=$((attempt + 1))[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4969770Z [36;1m    else[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4970620Z [36;1m      echo "Codesign failed after $max_attempts attempts for $target"[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4971710Z [36;1m      return 1[0m
2025-10-01T23:53:32.4972340Z [36;1m    fi[0m
